"<font size='4'>Unleash the Power of the Cosmic Cube</font><br><b>Setup</b>: 8 Twists.<br><b>Twist</b>: Put the Twist next to this Scheme.<br><b>Twist 5-6</b>: Each player gains a Wound.<br><b>Twist 7</b>: Each player gains 3 Wounds.<br><b>Twist 8</b>: Evil Wins!<br><br><br>"	Unleash the Power of the Cosmic Cube	B	Scheme
"<font size='4'>Capture Baby Hope</font><br><b>Setup</b>: 8 Twists. Put a token on this Scheme to represent the baby, Hope Summers.<br><b>Twist</b>: If a Villain has the baby, that Villain escapes. Otherwise, the baby is captured by the closest Villain to the Villain Deck. (If there are no Villains, do nothing.)<br><b>Special Rules</b>: The Villain with the baby gets +4 <img src=""Attack.jpg"" width=""16"">. If you defeat that Villain, rescue the baby to your Victory Pile (until the next Twist). The baby is worth 6 VP at the end of the game. If a Villain escapes with the baby, stack a Twist next to the Mastermind and return the baby to this Scheme card.<br><b>Evil Wins</b>: When there are 3 Twists stacked next to the Mastermind."	Capture Baby Hope	DC	Scheme
"<font size='4'>Detonate the Helicarrier</font><br><b>Setup</b>: 8 Twists. 6 Heroes in the Hero Deck.<br><b>Special Rules</b>: Whenever a Hero is KO'd from the HQ, turn that Hero face down on that HQ space, representing an Explosion on the Helicarrier. When an HQ space has 6 Explosions, that space is Destroyed and can't hold Heroes anymore.<br><b>Twist</b>: Stack this Twist next to the Scheme. Then for each Twist in that stack, KO the leftmost Hero in the HQ and immediately refill that space.<br><b>Evil Wins</b>: When all HQ spaces are Destroyed or the Hero Deck runs out."	Detonate the Helicarrier	DC	Scheme
